< Text>
So I guess I'm the odd one out here with all the stellar reviews this place is getting. I just moved to the SCV area and was in need of a go to barber place and picked Andy's because of their great reviews. However, the experience was one of the worst haircuts I have ever received. My barber was a women who spoke very little English and I'm pretty sure she didn't understand my request at all since I got something that resembled a wanna-be sloppy attempt at a rock-a-billy hair do. I had asked for a short clippers on the side with a high taper and one an a half inches on the top that was blended with the sides. What I received was of poor quality and lacked skill. She didn't even touch the hair at the front of my head and left it abnormally long. Long story short, I went to fantastic Sam's down the street and they fixed it for 10$ and said she was poorly skilled and lacked any real training, and was appalled that she was cutting hair. I would not recommend this place whatsoever. With that said,, it has a nice ambiance and with this being the beauty industry I know skill-set varies greatly from barber to barber. With that said she had first chair which indicated that she was one of their better barbers. I will not be returning and I recommend RJ at the Fantastic Sam's by Aldi down the street.< /Text>

< Review>
Love Village Fresh, always clean with helpful, friendly staff.  They actually bag your groceries and don't charge for the bag!  Meat selection is excellent and they have a cooked section that is impressive, tri tip burritos or sandwiches or whole cooked tri tip.  Chicken, teriyaki bowls, as well a vast variety or salads and pastas and cold sandwiches in deli.  Always fresh veggies and fruits as well as lots of yummy stuff from bakery.  They can get pricy but have good sales.  Milk is priced as low as they go when you buy 2 gallons. They sell Sees candy and lots if fun balloons and flowers.  Great ice cream selection and lots of hard to find speciality and local items.  Love my neighborhood Village Fresh!</Review>

<text>At one time the name was Richland Market, now its Village Fresh.  Best price on milk in town, as long as you buy 2 gallons.  Fantastic meats, and fresh produce.  However, the prices can be on the high end so if I have lots of shopping I usually skip here but for a quick few things like steaks and milk, this place is perfect.  They also specialize in hard to find items and locally made goods and wine.  Lots of organic items and a local, specialty dairy that bottles their milk in glass containers that you then return for the deposit.  Best strawberry and chocolate milk I ever tasted.  Other flavors like blueberry, banana, and various others as well.  Very clean, with knowledgeable, helpful staff.  Believe it or not they still bag your groceries here and will even help you out to your car!
Also feature a daily barbecue where you can put special orders in and have your meat done to your liking or grab a burrito on your lunch.  Also 2 daily fresh hot soups and many fresh items from bakery and deli.  Great seafood counter with lots of choices daily.  Fresh french bread daily and great sale prices on things every week.</text><Pics>None<//Pics><Response>None< /Response><GmapID>0x8091066af05fb895:0xf6b967f16487d5f3<//GmapID></record></dataset><record>

< Review>
Always friendly. Perfect neighborhood market. They really do attempt to provide variety. Just keep in mind you cannot always get a particular flavor in the brand you want. Example: diced tomatoes. They carry 4 or 5 brands but Del Monte might be no salt added, Hunt's may be certain flavors, S & W will be other flavors, etc... so if you are looking for a particular flavor and have a brand preference it gets complicated. Today I am trying Muir Glen diced tomatoes with Italian herbs because I do not care for S & W or Western Family, I like salt so no Del Monte, and I needed this flavor. I must say we have found new favorites this way.<//Review>

< review>
Passing through Turlock I heard about Village Fresh Market from a local.  I also heard it was a bit expensive but the prices were as good or better than some other typical cheaper grocery markets for the items I purchased.  The first things I noticed upon entering were the fresh produce displays and shortly thereafter the friendly staff members.  I saw several staff members and each one seemed happy to be at work helping customers.  The lady in the deli was especially nice and helpful, patient while I decided on a salad, and then showing me free utensils, napkins, etc. when I told her I was traveling.  The aisles were roomy and labeled well and the facility was clean.  I found every item I was looking for and checkout was a breeze.</review>

< Review>
As you guys know, I love sad malls and this one is no exception. The nostalgia is real. Even had some thin-railing'd stairs going to another floor but I didn't see where it went. Very clean as well, great atmosphere. Free wifi at Safeway with convenient bench to rest on. I'd recommend coming here for a quick trip back to the 90's. Even though I like calling old malls 'sad malls', this mall is anything but.<//Review>

< Review>
The Safeway & the Walgreens are the only real standout of this shopping plaza. The tiny 24 hour fitness is barely worth a mention as is the Chinese ready to eat restaurant inside. There is supposed to be a Subway moving into the plaza but I have not seen it yet. There are always panhandlers on the parking garage (Mason St) & Bay St. side but not the  Powell Street, but the staff that work there do not seem to really care about them. The gem in the plaza is the smokeshop next to the bathrooms.</Review>

This is not a good place at all. It feels like a run down mall, with lots of homeless people and people begging outside.
